1924: The Silent Decade

by ItsAstronomical

with the help of MassachusettsForStockdale, Lurker, River, and Gelid Lagopus

Sources

Calvin Coolidge, the GOP, and Teapot Dome

Calvin Coolidge is nothing short of an American Engima.
Despite my issues with him, he has often been misinterpreted by modern conservative commentators.
I hope this mod provides a better overview of his early administration and character.
We also ought to consider the party he served under and his predecessor's scandals he had to overcome.

Robert Sobel - Coolidge: An American Enigma
Amity Shlaes - Coolidge
William Edward Leuchtenburg - The Perils of Prosperity, 1914-32
J. Leonard Bates - The Teapot Dome Scandal and the Election of 1924
Robert James Maddox - Keeping Cool with Coolidge

John Davis and the Democratic Party

John Davis was a dark horse and a compromise candidate forced to be the sacrificial lamb for that year.
Nevertheless, he arguably represented the last breaths of an older type of Democrat.
To understand Davis and his position in 1924 is to understand the Democratic party at that point.
William Gibbs McAdoo was arguably the frontrunner for the nomination for awhile.
Therefore, research was done into how his campaign handled the convention.

Robert K. Murray - The 103rd Ballot
William Henry Harbaugh - Lawyer's lawyer; the life of John W. Davis
Philip M Chase - William Gibbs McAdoo: The last Progressive, (1863–1941)

Robert La Follette and the Progressive Movement

1924 was La Follette's last stand. He died the next year.
Therefore, this campaign is considered a sort of 'best hits' of his lifetime.
I included his autobiography here, of course with other sources as well.

Robert La Follette - La Follette's Autobiography; a personal narrative of political experiences
Richard Drake - The Education of an Anti-Imperialist: Robert La Follette and U.S. Expansion
Scott D. Johnston - Robert LaFollette and the Socialists

Sean Munger's YouTube Video

During my early work on this mod, I frequently recieved messages from people giving this 2-hour YouTube video as a source for the mod.
While getting all the twist-and-turns with CYOA required more information than one video can provide, I still reccomend this video!
I also do wanna thank everyone who sent me this. Your support is nice and it helps.

1924: The Silent Decade

by ItsAstronomical

with the help of MassachusettsForStockdale, Lurker, River, and Gelid Lagopus

Sources

Calvin Coolidge, the GOP, and Teapot Dome

Calvin Coolidge is nothing short of an American Engima.
Despite my issues with him, he has often been misinterpreted by modern conservative commentators.
I hope this mod provides a better overview of his early administration and character.
We also ought to consider the party he served under and his predecessor's scandals he had to overcome.

Robert Sobel - Coolidge: An American Enigma
Amity Shlaes - Coolidge
William Edward Leuchtenburg - The Perils of Prosperity, 1914-32
J. Leonard Bates - The Teapot Dome Scandal and the Election of 1924
Robert James Maddox - Keeping Cool with Coolidge

John Davis and the Democratic Party

John Davis was a dark horse and a compromise candidate forced to be the sacrificial lamb for that year.
Nevertheless, he arguably represented the last breaths of an older type of Democrat.
To understand Davis and his position in 1924 is to understand the Democratic party at that point.
William Gibbs McAdoo was arguably the frontrunner for the nomination for awhile.
Therefore, research was done into how his campaign handled the convention.

Robert K. Murray - The 103rd Ballot
William Henry Harbaugh - Lawyer's lawyer; the life of John W. Davis
Philip M Chase - William Gibbs McAdoo: The last Progressive, (1863–1941)

Robert La Follette and the Progressive Movement

1924 was La Follette's last stand. He died the next year.
Therefore, this campaign is considered a sort of 'best hits' of his lifetime.
I included his autobiography here, of course with other sources as well.

Robert La Follette - La Follette's Autobiography; a personal narrative of political experiences
Richard Drake - The Education of an Anti-Imperialist: Robert La Follette and U.S. Expansion
Scott D. Johnston - Robert LaFollette and the Socialists

Sean Munger's YouTube Video

During my early work on this mod, I frequently recieved messages from people giving this 2-hour YouTube video as a source for the mod.
While getting all the twist-and-turns with CYOA required more information than one video can provide, I still reccomend this video!
I also do wanna thank everyone who sent me this. Your support is nice and it helps.


Sean Munger - 1924: The Fascinating Forgotten Election

Special Thanks

This one took awhile, but I wanna thank all the playtesters. I appreciate it a bunch.
Mango helped with a couple coding things.
Lurker helped make a lot of outlines which made the writing process easier for me.
Thank you to Luuwuu for everything, obviously.
Oh, and of course...

...thank you for playing!

- Astronomical

1924: The Silent Decade

by ItsAstronomical

with the help of MassachusettsForStockdale, Lurker, River, and Gelid Lagopus

Sources

Calvin Coolidge, the GOP, and Teapot Dome

Calvin Coolidge is nothing short of an American Engima.
Despite my issues with him, he has often been misinterpreted by modern conservative commentators.
I hope this mod provides a better overview of his early administration and character.
We also ought to consider the party he served under and his predecessor's scandals he had to overcome.

Robert Sobel - Coolidge: An American Enigma
Amity Shlaes - Coolidge
William Edward Leuchtenburg - The Perils of Prosperity, 1914-32
J. Leonard Bates - The Teapot Dome Scandal and the Election of 1924
Robert James Maddox - Keeping Cool with Coolidge

John Davis and the Democratic Party

John Davis was a dark horse and a compromise candidate forced to be the sacrificial lamb for that year.
Nevertheless, he arguably represented the last breaths of an older type of Democrat.
To understand Davis and his position in 1924 is to understand the Democratic party at that point.
William Gibbs McAdoo was arguably the frontrunner for the nomination for awhile.
Therefore, research was done into how his campaign handled the convention.

Robert K. Murray - The 103rd Ballot
William Henry Harbaugh - Lawyer's lawyer; the life of John W. Davis
Philip M Chase - William Gibbs McAdoo: The last Progressive, (1863–1941)

Robert La Follette and the Progressive Movement

1924 was La Follette's last stand. He died the next year.
Therefore, this campaign is considered a sort of 'best hits' of his lifetime.
I included his autobiography here, of course with other sources as well.

Robert La Follette - La Follette's Autobiography; a personal narrative of political experiences
Richard Drake - The Education of an Anti-Imperialist: Robert La Follette and U.S. Expansion
Scott D. Johnston - Robert LaFollette and the Socialists

Sean Munger's YouTube Video

During my early work on this mod, I frequently recieved messages from people giving this 2-hour YouTube video as a source for the mod.
While getting all the twist-and-turns with CYOA required more information than one video can provide, I still reccomend this video!
I also do wanna thank everyone who sent me this. Your support is nice and it helps.


Sean Munger - 1924: The Fascinating Forgotten Election

Special Thanks

This one took awhile, but I wanna thank all the playtesters. I appreciate it a bunch.
Mango helped with a couple coding things.
Lurker helped make a lot of outlines which made the writing process easier for me.
Thank you to Luuwuu for everything, obviously.
Oh, and of course...

...thank you for playing!

- Astronomical
